## Workflow Orchestration

### 1. Plan Mode Default

- Enter plan mode for ANY non-trivial task (3+ steps or architectural decisions)
- If something goes sideways, STOP and re-plan immediately - don't keep pushing
- Use plan mode for verification steps, not just building
- Write detailed specs upfront to reduce ambiguity

### 2. Subagent Strategy

- Use subagents liberally to keep main context window clean
- Offload research, exploration, and parallel analysis to subagents
- For complex problems, throw more compute at it via subagents
- One task per subagent for focused execution

### 3. Self-Improvement Loop

- After ANY correction from the user: update tasks/lessons.md with the pattern
- Write rules for yourself that prevent the same mistake
- Ruthlessly iterate on these lessons until mistake rate drops
- Review lessons at session start for relevant project

### 4. Verification Before Done

- Never mark a task complete without proving it works
- Diff behavior between main and your changes when relevant
- Ask yourself: "Would a staff engineer approve this?"
- Run tests, check logs, demonstrate correctness

### 5. Demand Elegance (Balanced)

- For non-trivial changes: pause and ask "is there a more elegant way?"
- If a fix feels hacky: "Knowing everything I know now, implement the elegant solution"
- Skip this for simple, obvious fixes - don't over-engineer
- Challenge your own work before presenting it

### 6. Autonomous Bug Fixing

- When given a bug report: just fix it. Don't ask for hand-holding
- Point at logs, errors, failing tests - then resolve them
- Zero context switching required from the user
- Go fix failing CI tests without being told how
- You can run tests in tmp folder after every feature you add to make sure they work as expected or not.

## Task Management

1. Plan First: Write plan to tasks/todo.md with checkable items
2. Verify Plan: Check in before starting implementation
3. Track Progress: Mark items complete as you go
4. Explain Changes: High-level summary at each step
5. Document Results: Add review section to tasks/todo.md
6. Capture Lessons: Update tasks/lessons.md after corrections

## Core Principles

- Simplicity First: Make every change as simple as possible. Impact minimal code.
- No Laziness: Find root causes. No temporary fixes. Senior developer standards.
- Minimal Impact: Changes should only touch what's necessary. Avoid introducing bugs.
--- lessons
# Lessons Learned

## Session Lessons
- Supabase paused projects block schema dumps and linking operations.
- For this environment, Supabase direct DB hosts resolved to IPv6 and failed; pooler endpoints worked.
- For type generation, use Supabase CLI with project ref: `supabase gen types typescript --project-id <ref> --schema public > src/types/supabase.ts`.
- Avoid `supabase gen types --db-url ...` in this environment; it attempted a Docker-backed path and failed when Docker daemon was unavailable.
- Raw `pg_dump` output is not fully idempotent on Supabase; `CREATE SCHEMA` and `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES` can fail.
- Applying dumps to Supabase requires filtering unsupported privilege statements.
- DB-first migrations can break app runtime immediately when code still references removed tables/columns.
- Cloudflare global API key must use `X-Auth-Key` + `X-Auth-Email`, not Bearer token.
- R2 bucket creation via API is straightforward, but S3 key management differs from API token handling.
- Always validate new R2 credentials with a real S3 request before using them in production envs.
- Keep `tasks/` ignored by default but force-add specific planning files when needed.
- When user is editing concurrently, avoid touching their changed files and commit only explicit pathspecs.
- When running Vitest with configs under `tests/`, execute from the `tests/` working directory (or adjust paths) so `setup.ts` resolves correctly.
- Vitest v4 constructor mocks must provide constructable implementations for class-like dependencies (for example, `new Resend(...)`).
- During gateway/OTP deprecations, remove stale route/service tests first, then re-baseline middleware and payment-flow assertions to current endpoints.
- Keep `tests/.env` synchronized with root env profile keys (including key-name mappings like publishable key aliases) before trusting test-suite results.

## Implementation Guardrails
- Keep schema and generated types in lockstep.
- Prefer `--project-id` generation from Supabase CLI as the default regeneration method for `src/types/supabase.ts`.
- Make payment callbacks idempotent before enabling live traffic.
- Use preview-first rollout with explicit drift checks between preview and production.
- Maintain a single migration runbook with exact commands and expected outputs.
- Keep deploy workflow env blocks aligned with active providers; stale secret keys in CI can silently rot release readiness.
- Prefer behavior-driven test expectations from current route/service contracts; update brittle response/message assertions immediately after contract changes.
- When Next.js route handlers accept `NextRequest`, integration/unit tests must call handlers with a request object; `GET()` without args can produce false 500 failures.
- For integrations touching third-party APIs (email/SMS), gate strict success assertions behind real credential detection and validate graceful fallback behavior for placeholder/local configs.

     1	'use client';
     2	
     3	import { useState, useMemo, memo, useEffect } from 'react';
     4	import ProductCard from './ProductCard';

    11	
    12	export type ProductSortOption =
    13	  | 'popular'
    14	  | 'price-asc'
    15	  | 'price-desc'
    16	  | 'featured'
    17	  | 'discount'
    18	  | 'newest';
    19	
    20	interface Variant {
    21	  id: string;
    22	  name: string;
    23	  color?: string | null;
    24	  size?: string | null;
    25	  material?: string | null;
    26	  priceAdjust: number;
    27	  stock: number;
    28	  isActive: boolean;
    29	  createdAt?: string;
    30	  media?: Array<{
    31	    id: string;
    32	    type: 'IMAGE' | 'VIDEO';
    33	    url: string;
    34	    alt?: string | null;
    35	    order: number;
    36	  }>;
    37	}
    38	
    39	interface Product {
    40	  id: string;
    41	  name: string;
    42	  description: string;
    43	  price: number;
    44	  discountPercent?: number | null;
    45	  stock: number;
    46	  images: string[];
    47	  isActive: boolean;
    48	  isFeatured?: boolean;
    49	  hasVariants?: boolean;
    50	  variants?: Variant[];
    51	  createdAt?: string;
    52	  displayOrder: number;
    53	}
    54	
    55	interface ProductListProps {
    56	  initialProducts?: Product[];
    57	  initialPage?: number;
    58	  initialTotal?: number;
    59	}
    60	
    61	/**
    62	 * Client-side sorting function
    63	 * Sorts products based on the selected option WITHOUT making API calls
    64	 * This makes filtering instant and reduces server load
    65	 */
    66	function sortProducts(
    67	  products: Product[],
    68	  sortBy: ProductSortOption
    69	): Product[] {
    70	  const sorted = [...products];
    71	
    72	  switch (sortBy) {
    73	    case 'popular':
    74	      // Popular: Sort by displayOrder (ascending), then by createdAt (newest first)
    75	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
    76	        if (a.displayOrder !== b.displayOrder) {
    77	          return a.displayOrder - b.displayOrder;
    78	        }
    79	        if (!a.createdAt || !b.createdAt) return 0;
    80	        return (
    81	          new Date(b.createdAt).getTime() - new Date(a.createdAt).getTime()
    82	        );
    83	      });
    84	
    85	    case 'price-asc':
    86	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price);
    87	
    88	    case 'price-desc':
    89	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.price - a.price);
    90	
    91	    case 'featured':
    92	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
    93	        // Featured first
    94	        if (a.isFeatured && !b.isFeatured) return -1;
    95	        if (!a.isFeatured && b.isFeatured) return 1;
    96	        return 0;
    97	      });
    98	
    99	    case 'discount':
   100	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
   101	        const aDiscount = a.discountPercent || 0;
   102	        const bDiscount = b.discountPercent || 0;
   103	        return bDiscount - aDiscount;
   104	      });
   105	
   106	    case 'newest':
   107	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
   108	        if (!a.createdAt || !b.createdAt) return 0;
   109	        return (
   110	          new Date(b.createdAt).getTime() - new Date(a.createdAt).getTime()
   111	        );
   112	      });
   113	
   114	    default:
   115	      // Fallback to popular
   116	      return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
   117	        if (a.displayOrder !== b.displayOrder) {
   118	          return a.displayOrder - b.displayOrder;
   119	        }
   120	        if (!a.createdAt || !b.createdAt) return 0;
   121	        return (
   122	          new Date(b.createdAt).getTime() - new Date(a.createdAt).getTime()
   123	        );
   124	      });
   125	  }
   126	}
   127	
   128	function ProductList({
   129	  initialProducts = [],
   130	  initialPage = 1,
   131	  initialTotal = 0,
   132	}: ProductListProps) {
   133	  // Store ALL products fetched from server
   134	  const [allProducts, setAllProducts] = useState<Product[]>(initialProducts);
   135	  const [isInitialLoad, setIsInitialLoad] = useState(true);
   136	  const [page, setPage] = useState(initialPage);
   137	  const [total] = useState(initialTotal); // Only used for initial fetch calculation
   138	  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
   139	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
   140	  const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState<ProductSortOption>('popular');
   141	  const { rateLimitInfo, clearRateLimit, fetchWithRateLimit } =
   142	    useApiWithRateLimit();
   143	  const perPage = 20;
   144	
   145	  // Fetch ALL products on mount (only once)
   146	  useEffect(() => {
   147	    if (isInitialLoad && allProducts.length < total) {
   148	      // Calculate how many pages we need to fetch to get all products
   149	      const totalPages = Math.ceil(total / perPage);
   150	
   151	      const fetchAllProducts = async () => {
   152	        setIsLoading(true);
   153	        try {
   154	          // Fetch remaining pages
   155	          const pagePromises = [];
   156	          for (let i = 2; i <= totalPages; i++) {
   157	            pagePromises.push(
   158	              fetchWithRateLimit<{ data: Product[]; total: number }>(() =>
   159	                fetch(
   160	                  `/api/products?page=${i}&perPage=${perPage}&sortBy=popular`
   161	                )
   162	              )
   163	            );
   164	          }
   165	
   166	          const results = await Promise.all(pagePromises);
   167	          const additionalProducts = results.flatMap((r) => r?.data || []);
   168	
   169	          setAllProducts([...initialProducts, ...additionalProducts]);
   170	        } catch (err) {
   171	          console.error('Error fetching all products:', err);
   172	          // Keep using initial products if fetch fails
   173	        } finally {
   174	          setIsLoading(false);
   175	          setIsInitialLoad(false);
   176	        }
   177	      };
   178	
   179	      // Only fetch if we have more than one page
   180	      if (totalPages > 1) {
   181	        fetchAllProducts();
   182	      } else {
   183	        setIsInitialLoad(false);
   184	      }
   185	    } else {
   186	      setIsInitialLoad(false);
   187	    }
   188	  }, [
   189	    total,
   190	    perPage,
   191	    initialProducts,
   192	    isInitialLoad,
   193	    allProducts.length,
   194	    fetchWithRateLimit,
   195	  ]);
   196	
   197	  // Client-side sorted products (instant filtering!)
   198	  const sortedProducts = useMemo(() => {
   199	    return sortProducts(allProducts, sortBy);
   200	  }, [allProducts, sortBy]);
   201	
   202	  // Paginate sorted products client-side
   203	  const paginatedProducts = useMemo(() => {
   204	    const startIndex = (page - 1) * perPage;
   205	    const endIndex = startIndex + perPage;
   206	    return sortedProducts.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
   207	  }, [sortedProducts, page, perPage]);
   208	
   209	  const totalPages = Math.ceil(sortedProducts.length / perPage);
   210	
   211	  // Memoize pagination page numbers calculation
   212	  const pageNumbers = useMemo(() => {
   213	    const maxPages = Math.min(totalPages, 5);
   214	    return Array.from({ length: maxPages }, (_, i) => {
   215	      if (totalPages <= 5) {
   216	        return i + 1;
   217	      } else if (page <= 3) {
   218	        return i + 1;
   219	      } else if (page >= totalPages - 2) {
   220	        return totalPages - 4 + i;
   221	      } else {
   222	        return page - 2 + i;
   223	      }
   224	    });
   225	  }, [totalPages, page]);
   226	
   227	  const handlePageChange = (newPage: number) => {
   228	    // Validate page number
   229	    if (newPage < 1 || newPage > totalPages) {
   230	      return;
   231	    }
   232	
   233	    // Don't change if already on that page
   234	    if (newPage === page) {
   235	      return;
   236	    }
   237	
   238	    setPage(newPage);
   239	    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
   240	  };
   241	
   242	  const handleSortChange = (newSort: ProductSortOption) => {
   243	    if (newSort === sortBy) return;
   244	    setSortBy(newSort);
   245	    setPage(1); // Reset to first page when sorting changes
   246	    // No API call needed - sorting happens instantly on client!
   247	  };
   248	
   249	  if (paginatedProducts.length === 0 && !isLoading) {
   250	    return (
   251	      <div className="py-12 text-center">
   252	        <div className="mb-2 text-lg text-slate-700">No products found</div>
   253	        <p className="text-slate-500">
   254	          There are no products available for this view.
   255	        </p>
   256	      </div>
   257	    );
   258	  }
   259	
   260	  return (
   261	    <div>
   262	      {/* Rate Limit Error */}
   263	      {rateLimitInfo.isRateLimited && rateLimitInfo.retryAfter && (
   264	        <RateLimitError
   265	          retryAfter={rateLimitInfo.retryAfter}
   266	          onRetryReady={clearRateLimit}
   267	          className="mb-6"
   268	        />
   269	      )}
   270	
   271	      {/* General Error */}
   272	      {error && (
   273	        <Alert type="error" className="mb-6" onClose={() => setError(null)}>
   274	          {error}
   275	        </Alert>
   276	      )}
   277	
   278	      {/* Sort Controls */}
   279	      <div className="mb-6 flex justify-end">
   280	        <div className="w-full sm:w-64">
   281	          <Select
   282	            value={sortBy}
   283	            onChange={(value) => handleSortChange(value as ProductSortOption)}
   284	            label="Sort by"
   285	            options={[
   286	              { value: 'popular', label: 'Popular' },
   287	              { value: 'newest', label: 'Newest' },
   288	              { value: 'price-asc', label: 'Price: low to high' },
   289	              { value: 'price-desc', label: 'Price: high to low' },
   290	              { value: 'featured', label: 'Featured' },
   291	              { value: 'discount', label: 'Best discount' },
   292	            ]}
   293	          />
   294	        </div>
   295	      </div>
   296	
   297	      {/* Products Grid */}
   298	      {isLoading && isInitialLoad ? (
   299	        <ProductCardSkeletonGrid count={perPage} />
   300	      ) : (
   301	        <>
   302	          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6 mb-8">
   303	            {paginatedProducts.map((product) => (
   304	              <ProductCard key={product.id} product={product} />
   305	            ))}
   306	          </div>
   307	
   308	          {/* Pagination */}
   309	          {totalPages > 1 && (
   310	            <div className="flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   311	              <Button
   312	                variant="secondary"
   313	                size="sm"
   314	                disabled={page === 1}
   315	                onClick={() => handlePageChange(page - 1)}
   316	              >
   317	                Previous
   318	              </Button>
   319	
   320	              <div className="flex items-center gap-1">

--- v4
'use client';

import { ButtonHTMLAttributes, ReactNode, forwardRef } from 'react';

export interface ButtonV4Props extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger' | 'soft';
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  isLoading?: boolean;
  icon?: ReactNode;
  iconPosition?: 'start' | 'end';
  fullWidth?: boolean;
  rounded?: 'default' | 'full';
  children: ReactNode;
}

const ButtonV4 = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonV4Props>(
  (
    {
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      icon,
      iconPosition = 'start',
      fullWidth = false,
      rounded = 'default',
      children,
      disabled,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const baseStyles = `
      inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2
      font-semibold
      transition-colors duration-200 ease-out
      focus:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:ring-offset-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-background
      disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:pointer-events-none
      select-none
    `;

    const variantStyles = {
      primary: 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90',
      secondary:
        'bg-card text-foreground border border-border hover:bg-muted dark:bg-card dark:hover:bg-muted',
      outline:
        'bg-transparent text-foreground border border-border hover:bg-muted',
      ghost: 'bg-transparent text-foreground hover:bg-muted',
      danger: 'bg-danger text-danger-foreground hover:bg-danger/90',
      soft: 'bg-primary-muted text-foreground border border-transparent hover:bg-primary-muted/80 dark:text-foreground',
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      sm: 'h-9 px-3 text-xs',
      md: 'h-10 px-4 text-sm',
      lg: 'h-11 px-5 text-base',
    };

    const roundedStyles = {
      default: 'rounded-lg',
      full: 'rounded-full',
    };

    const LoadingSpinner = () => (
      <svg
        className="h-4 w-4 animate-spin"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        fill="none"
        viewBox="0 0 24 24"
        aria-hidden="true"
      >
        <circle
          className="opacity-25"
          cx="12"
          cy="12"
          r="10"
          stroke="currentColor"
          strokeWidth="3"
        />
        <path
          className="opacity-75"
          fill="currentColor"
          d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
        />
      </svg>
    );

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        disabled={disabled || isLoading}
        aria-busy={isLoading || undefined}
        className={`
          ${baseStyles}
          ${variantStyles[variant]}
          ${sizeStyles[size]}
          ${roundedStyles[rounded]}
          ${fullWidth ? 'w-full' : ''}
          ${className}
        `}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading ? (
          <>
            <LoadingSpinner />
            <span>Loading...</span>
          </>
        ) : (
          <>
            {icon && iconPosition === 'start' && (
              <span className="flex-shrink-0">{icon}</span>
            )}
            {children}
            {icon && iconPosition === 'end' && (
              <span className="flex-shrink-0">{icon}</span>
            )}
          </>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

ButtonV4.displayName = 'ButtonV4';

export default ButtonV4;

    32	}
    33	
    34	interface ProductCardProps {
    35	  product: {
    36	    id: string;
    37	    name: string;
    38	    description: string;
    39	    price: number;
    40	    discountPercent?: number | null;
    41	    stock: number;
    42	    images: string[];
    43	    isActive: boolean;
    44	    isFeatured?: boolean;
    45	    hasVariants?: boolean;
    46	    variants?: Variant[];
    47	  };
    48	}
    49	
    50	function ProductCard({ product }: ProductCardProps) {
    51	  const addItem = useCartStore((state) => state.addItem);
    52	  const router = useRouter();
    53	  const [isAdding, setIsAdding] = useState(false);
    54	
    55	  // Get active variants - memoized to prevent dependency changes on every render
    56	  const activeVariants = useMemo(
    57	    () => product.variants?.filter((v) => v.isActive) || [],
    58	    [product.variants]
    59	  );
    60	  const hasVariants = product.hasVariants && activeVariants.length > 0;
    61	
    62	  // Auto-select first active variant with media if available
    63	  const getDefaultVariant = (): Variant | null => {
    64	    if (!hasVariants) return null;
    65	
    66	    // Prefer variant with media
    67	    const variantWithMedia = activeVariants.find(
    68	      (v) => v.media && v.media.length > 0
    69	    );
    70	    if (variantWithMedia) return variantWithMedia;
    71	
    72	    // Fallback to first active variant
    73	    return activeVariants[0] || null;
    74	  };
    75	
    76	  const defaultVariant = getDefaultVariant();
    77	  const [selectedVariant, setSelectedVariant] = useState<Variant | null>(
    78	    defaultVariant
    79	  );
    80	
    81	  // Set initial image based on default variant or product images
    82	  const getInitialImage = () => {
    83	    if (defaultVariant?.media && defaultVariant.media.length > 0) {
    84	      return defaultVariant.media[0].url;
    85	    }
    86	    return product.images[0] || '';
    87	  };
    88	
    89	  const [currentImage, setCurrentImage] = useState(getInitialImage());
    90	
    91	  // Get color variants for image swapping
    92	  const colorVariants = useMemo(() => {
    93	    return activeVariants.filter(
    94	      (v) => v.color && v.media && v.media.length > 0
    95	    );
    96	  }, [activeVariants]);
    97	
    98	  const hasColorVariants = colorVariants.length > 1;
    99	
   100	  // Current variant index for carousel
   101	  const [currentVariantIndex, setCurrentVariantIndex] = useState(() => {
   102	    if (!hasColorVariants) return 0;
   103	    const index = colorVariants.findIndex((v) => v.id === selectedVariant?.id);
   104	    return index >= 0 ? index : 0;
   105	  });
   106	
   107	  // Touch swipe handling
   108	  const touchStartX = useRef<number>(0);
   109	  const touchEndX = useRef<number>(0);
   110	  const minSwipeDistance = 50; // Minimum swipe distance in pixels
   111	
   112	  // Track preloaded variant images
   113	  const preloadedVariants = useRef<Set<string>>(new Set());
   114	
   115	  // PRELOADING STRATEGY: Aggressively preload all color variant images on mount
   116	  // This ensures instant switching when user swipes between variants
   117	  useEffect(() => {
   118	    if (!hasColorVariants || colorVariants.length === 0) return;
   119	
   120	    // Preload all color variant images
   121	    colorVariants.forEach((variant, index) => {
   122	      if (preloadedVariants.current.has(variant.id)) return; // Skip if already preloaded
   123	
   124	      const isFirstVariant = index === 0;
   125	      const variantImages =
   126	        variant.media?.filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE') || [];
   127	
   128	      variantImages.forEach((media, mediaIndex) => {
   129	        const isFirstImage = mediaIndex === 0;
   130	        const priority =
   131	          isFirstVariant && isFirstImage ? 1 : isFirstImage ? 2 : 3;
   132	
   133	        const preloadFn = () => {
   134	          const img = new window.Image();
   135	          img.src = optimizeImage.thumbnail(media.url);
   136	          if (priority <= 2) {
   137	            img.fetchPriority = 'high';
   138	          }
   139	        };
   140	
   141	        // High-priority images load immediately, low-priority during idle time
   142	        if (priority <= 2) {
   143	          preloadFn();
   144	        } else {
   145	          if (
   146	            typeof window !== 'undefined' &&
   147	            'requestIdleCallback' in window
   148	          ) {
   149	            window.requestIdleCallback(preloadFn);
   150	          } else {
   151	            setTimeout(preloadFn, 100);
   152	          }
   153	        }
   154	      });
   155	
   156	      preloadedVariants.current.add(variant.id);
   157	    });
   158	  }, [hasColorVariants, colorVariants]);
   159	
   160	  // Navigate to next color variant image
   161	  const goToNextVariant = useCallback(() => {
   162	    if (!hasColorVariants) return;
   163	
   164	    const nextIndex = (currentVariantIndex + 1) % colorVariants.length;
   165	    setCurrentVariantIndex(nextIndex);
   166	    const nextVariant = colorVariants[nextIndex];
   167	    setSelectedVariant(nextVariant);
   168	    if (nextVariant.media && nextVariant.media.length > 0) {
   169	      setCurrentImage(nextVariant.media[0].url);
   170	    }
   171	  }, [hasColorVariants, currentVariantIndex, colorVariants]);
   172	
   173	  // Navigate to previous color variant image
   174	  const goToPrevVariant = useCallback(() => {
   175	    if (!hasColorVariants) return;
   176	
   177	    const prevIndex =
   178	      currentVariantIndex === 0
   179	        ? colorVariants.length - 1
   180	        : currentVariantIndex - 1;
   181	    setCurrentVariantIndex(prevIndex);
   182	    const prevVariant = colorVariants[prevIndex];
   183	    setSelectedVariant(prevVariant);
   184	    if (prevVariant.media && prevVariant.media.length > 0) {
   185	      setCurrentImage(prevVariant.media[0].url);
   186	    }
   187	  }, [hasColorVariants, currentVariantIndex, colorVariants]);
   188	
   189	  // Touch swipe handlers
   190	  const onTouchStart = useCallback(
   191	    (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   192	      if (!hasColorVariants) return;
   193	      touchEndX.current = 0; // Reset
   194	      touchStartX.current = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
   195	    },
   196	    [hasColorVariants]
   197	  );
   198	
   199	  const onTouchMove = useCallback(
   200	    (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   201	      if (!hasColorVariants) return;
   202	      touchEndX.current = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
   203	    },
   204	    [hasColorVariants]
   205	  );
   206	
   207	  const onTouchEnd = useCallback(
   208	    (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   209	      if (!hasColorVariants) return;
   210	      if (!touchStartX.current || !touchEndX.current) return;
   211	
   212	      const distance = touchStartX.current - touchEndX.current;
   213	      const isLeftSwipe = distance > minSwipeDistance;
   214	      const isRightSwipe = distance < -minSwipeDistance;
   215	
   216	      // In RTL, left swipe = next, right swipe = previous
   217	      if (isLeftSwipe) {
   218	        e.preventDefault();
   219	        e.stopPropagation();
   220	        goToNextVariant();
   221	      } else if (isRightSwipe) {
   222	        e.preventDefault();
   223	        e.stopPropagation();
   224	        goToPrevVariant();
   225	      }
   226	
   227	      // Reset
   228	      touchStartX.current = 0;
   229	      touchEndX.current = 0;
   230	    },
   231	    [hasColorVariants, goToNextVariant, goToPrevVariant]
   232	  );
   233	
   234	  // Calculate discounted price
   235	  const discountPercent = product.discountPercent || 0;
   236	  const basePrice = Number(product.price);
   237	  const effectivePrice = selectedVariant
   238	    ? basePrice + Number(selectedVariant.priceAdjust)
   239	    : basePrice;
   240	  const discountedPrice =
   241	    discountPercent > 0
   242	      ? effectivePrice * (1 - discountPercent / 100)
   243	      : effectivePrice;
   244	
   245	  // Effective stock considering variant selection
   246	  const effectiveStock = selectedVariant
   247	    ? selectedVariant.stock
   248	    : product.stock;
   249	  const isOutOfStock = effectiveStock === 0;
   250	
   251	  const handleVariantSelect = (variant: Variant) => {
   252	    setSelectedVariant(variant);
   253	
   254	    // Update image when variant is selected
   255	    if (variant.media && variant.media.length > 0) {
   256	      setCurrentImage(variant.media[0].url);
   257	    } else {
   258	      // Fallback to product's first image
   259	      setCurrentImage(product.images[0] || '');
   260	    }
   261	
   262	    // Update carousel index if this is a color variant
   263	    if (hasColorVariants && variant.color) {
   264	      const variantIndex = colorVariants.findIndex((v) => v.id === variant.id);
   265	      if (variantIndex >= 0) {
   266	        setCurrentVariantIndex(variantIndex);
   267	      }
   268	    }
   269	  };
   270	
   271	  const handleAddToCart = useCallback(async () => {
   272	    try {
   273	      // If product has variants, variant selection is REQUIRED
   274	      if (hasVariants && !selectedVariant) {
   275	        toast.warning('Select a product option first');
   276	        return;
   277	      }
   278	
   279	      setIsAdding(true);
   280	      addItem(
   281	        {
   282	          productId: product.id,
   283	          name: selectedVariant
   284	            ? `${product.name} - ${selectedVariant.name}`
   285	            : product.name,
   286	          price: discountedPrice,
   287	          image: currentImage,
   288	          stock: effectiveStock,
   289	          variantId: selectedVariant?.id,
   290	          variantName: selectedVariant?.name,
   291	        },
   292	        1
   293	      );
   294	      // Show success feedback and offer checkout
   295	      setTimeout(() => {
   296	        setIsAdding(false);
   297	        toast.success('Product added to cart', {
   298	          action: {
   299	            label: 'Go to checkout',
   300	            onClick: () => router.push('/checkout'),
   301	          },
   302	        });
   303	      }, 300);
   304	    } catch (error) {
   305	      toast.error(
   306	        error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Could not add product to cart'
   307	      );
   308	      setIsAdding(false);
   309	    }
   310	  }, [
   311	    product.id,
   312	    product.name,
   313	    hasVariants,
   314	    selectedVariant,
   315	    discountedPrice,
   316	    currentImage,
   317	    effectiveStock,
   318	    addItem,
   319	    router,
   320	  ]);
   321	
   322	  return (
   323	    <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-sm transition-all hover:-translate-y-1 hover:shadow-md dark:border-slate-800 dark:bg-slate-900">
   324	      {/* Product Image */}
   325	      <Link href={`/products/${product.id}`}>
   326	        <div
   327	          className="group relative aspect-[4/5] w-full overflow-hidden bg-slate-100 dark:bg-slate-800"
   328	          onTouchStart={onTouchStart}
   329	          onTouchMove={onTouchMove}
   330	          onTouchEnd={onTouchEnd}
   331	        >
   332	          {currentImage ? (
   333	            <Image
   334	              src={optimizeImage.thumbnail(currentImage)}
   335	              alt={generateProductAltText({
   336	                productName: product.name,
   337	                variantName: selectedVariant?.name,
   338	                color: selectedVariant?.color,
   339	                size: selectedVariant?.size,
   340	                material: selectedVariant?.material,
   341	              })}
   342	              fill
   343	              loading="lazy"
   344	              className="object-cover object-center hover:scale-105 transition-transform duration-300"
   345	              sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, (max-width: 768px) 50vw, (max-width: 1024px) 33vw, 25vw"
   346	            />
   347	          ) : (
   348	            <div className="flex h-full w-full items-center justify-center">
   349	              <div className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-400">No image</div>
   350	            </div>
   351	          )}
   352	          {/* Wishlist Button - Left side (RTL: visually on right) */}
   353	          <div className="absolute left-2 top-2 z-10">
   354	            <WishlistButton
   355	              product={{
   356	                id: product.id,
   357	                name: product.name,
   358	                price: discountedPrice,
   359	                images: product.images,
   360	                stock: effectiveStock,
   361	                discountPercent: product.discountPercent,
   362	              }}
   363	              variant={
   364	                selectedVariant
   365	                  ? {
   366	                      id: selectedVariant.id,
   367	                      name: selectedVariant.name,
   368	                      media: selectedVariant.media,
   369	                    }
   370	                  : null
   371	              }
   372	              size="md"
   373	              className="bg-white/90 shadow-sm backdrop-blur-sm"
   374	            />
   375	          </div>
   376	          {/* Badges */}
   377	          <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 flex flex-col gap-2">
   378	            {product.isFeatured && (
   379	              <Badge variant="premium" size="sm">
   380	                Featured
   381	              </Badge>
   382	            )}
   383	            {discountPercent > 0 && (
   384	              <Badge variant="error" size="sm">
   385	                {discountPercent}% off
   386	              </Badge>
   387	            )}
   388	          </div>
   389	          {isOutOfStock && (
   390	            <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/55">
   391	              <span className="text-lg font-bold text-white">Out of stock</span>
   392	            </div>
   393	          )}
   394	        </div>
   395	      </Link>
   396	
   397	      {/* Product Info */}
   398	      <div className="space-y-3 p-4">
   399	        <p className="line-clamp-1 text-xs text-slate-500">
   400	          {product.description}
   401	        </p>
   402	        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
   403	          {discountPercent > 0 && (
   404	            <Badge variant="error" size="sm">
   405	              Sale
   406	            </Badge>
   407	          )}
   408	          {product.isFeatured && (
   409	            <Badge variant="premium" size="sm">
   410	              Featured
   411	            </Badge>
   412	          )}
   413	        </div>
   414	        <Link href={`/products/${product.id}`}>
   415	          <h3 className="line-clamp-2 text-base font-semibold text-slate-950 hover:text-blue-700 dark:text-white dark:hover:text-blue-300">
   416	            {product.name}
   417	          </h3>
   418	        </Link>
   419	
   420	        {/* Variant Selector - Compact Version for Cards */}
   421	        {hasVariants && (
   422	          <div className="space-y-2">
   423	            {colorVariants.length > 0 && (
   424	              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
   425	                {colorVariants.map((variant) => {
   426	                  const isSelected = selectedVariant?.id === variant.id;
   427	                  const variantOutOfStock = variant.stock === 0;
   428	
   429	                  return (
   430	                    <button
   431	                      key={variant.id}
   432	                      onClick={(e) => {
   433	                        e.preventDefault();
   434	                        if (!variantOutOfStock) handleVariantSelect(variant);
   435	                      }}
   436	                      disabled={variantOutOfStock}
   437	                      className={`relative h-6 w-6 rounded-lg border transition-all ${
   438	                        isSelected
   439	                          ? 'border-blue-600 ring-2 ring-blue-200/70'
   440	                          : 'border-slate-200 hover:border-slate-300'
   441	                      } ${variantOutOfStock ? 'opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed' : 'cursor-pointer'}`}
   442	                      title={variantOutOfStock ? 'Out of stock' : variant.name}
   443	                      aria-label={variant.name}
   444	                    >
   445	                      <span
   446	                        className="absolute inset-0 rounded-[6px] border border-white/70"
   447	                        style={{ background: variant.color || '#e2e8f0' }}
   448	                      />
   449	                    </button>
   450	                  );
   451	                })}
   452	              </div>
   453	            )}
   454	
   455	            {activeVariants.some((variant) => !variant.color) && (
   456	              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
   457	                {activeVariants
   458	                  .filter((variant) => !variant.color)
   459	                  .map((variant) => {
   460	                    const isSelected = selectedVariant?.id === variant.id;
   461	                    const variantOutOfStock = variant.stock === 0;
   462	                    const label =
   463	                      variant.size || variant.material || variant.name;
   464	
   465	                    return (
   466	                      <button
   467	                        key={variant.id}
   468	                        onClick={(e) => {
   469	                          e.preventDefault();
   470	                          if (!variantOutOfStock) handleVariantSelect(variant);
   471	                        }}
   472	                        disabled={variantOutOfStock}
   473	                        className={`px-2.5 py-1 text-xs rounded-full border transition-all ${
   474	                          isSelected
   475	                            ? 'border-blue-600 bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 font-medium'
   476	                            : 'border-slate-200 hover:border-slate-300 text-slate-600'
   477	                        } ${variantOutOfStock ? 'opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed line-through' : 'cursor-pointer'}`}
   478	                        title={
   479	                          variantOutOfStock ? 'Out of stock' : variant.name
   480	                        }
   481	                      >
   482	                        {label}
   483	                      </button>
   484	                    );
   485	                  })}
   486	              </div>
   487	            )}
   488	          </div>
   489	        )}
   490	
   491	        {/* Price */}
   492	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   493	          {discountPercent > 0 ? (
   494	            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   495	              <span className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950 dark:text-white">
   496	                {formatPrice(discountedPrice)}
   497	              </span>
   498	              <span className="text-sm text-slate-400 line-through">
   499	                {formatPrice(effectivePrice)}
   500	              </span>
   501	            </div>
   502	          ) : (
   503	            <span className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950 dark:text-white">
   504	              {formatPrice(effectivePrice)}
   505	            </span>
   506	          )}
   507	        </div>
   508	
   509	        {/* Add to Cart Button */}
   510	        <Button
   511	          variant="primary"
   512	          size="md"
   513	          className="w-full"
   514	          disabled={isOutOfStock}
   515	          isLoading={isAdding}
   516	          onClick={handleAddToCart}
   517	        >
   518	          {isOutOfStock
   519	            ? 'Out of stock'
   520	            : isAdding
   521	              ? 'Adding...'
   522	              : 'Add to Cart'}
   523	        </Button>
   524	      </div>
   525	    </div>
   526	  );
   527	}
   528	
   529	export default memo(ProductCard);

   428

export type SiteDirection = 'ltr' | 'rtl';

function getDirection(value: string | undefined): SiteDirection {
  return value === 'rtl' ? 'rtl' : 'ltr';
}

export const siteConfig = {
  name: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_NAME || 'Supabase Vercel Stack',

    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_DESCRIPTION ||
    'Open-source commerce boilerplate for Supabase and Vercel.',

  locale: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_LOCALE || 'en-US',

};

src/lib/utils/format.ts:3:export function formatPrice(price: number): string {
import { siteLocale } from '@/config/site';

export function formatPrice(price: number): string {
  return new Intl.NumberFormat(siteLocale.locale, {
    style: 'currency',
    currency: siteLocale.currency,
  }).format(price);
}

export function formatNumber(value: number): string {
  return new Intl.NumberFormat(siteLocale.locale).format(value);
}

export function formatDate(
  value: Date | string | number,
  options: Intl.DateTimeFormatOptions = {}
): string {
  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat(siteLocale.locale, {
    year: 'numeric',
    month: '2-digit',
    day: '2-digit',
    timeZone: siteLocale.timeZone,
    ...options,
  }).format(new Date(value));
}

export function formatDateTime(value: Date | string | number): string {
  return formatDate(value, {
    hour: '2-digit',
    minute: '2-digit',
  });
}

/**
 * Calculate discounted price
 */
export function calculateDiscountedPrice(
  basePrice: number,
  discountPercent: number | null | undefined
): number {
  if (!discountPercent || discountPercent <= 0) {
    return basePrice;
  }
  return basePrice * (1 - discountPercent / 100);
}

import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';
import { createBrowserStorage } from '@/lib/browser-storage';
import { formatPrice as formatStorefrontPrice } from '@/lib/utils/format';

export interface CartItem {
  productId: string;
  name: string;
  price: number;
  quantity: number;
  image: string;
  stock: number;
  variantId?: string;
  variantName?: string;
}

interface CartStore {
  items: CartItem[];
  addItem: (product: Omit<CartItem, 'quantity'>, quantity: number) => void;
  removeItem: (productId: string, variantId?: string) => void;
  removeUnavailableItems: (productIds: string[]) => void;
  updateQuantity: (
    productId: string,
    quantity: number,
    variantId?: string
  ) => void;
  clearCart: () => void;
  total: number;
  itemCount: number;
}

export const useCartStore = create<CartStore>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      items: [],

      addItem: (product, quantity) => {
        const { items } = get();
        // Match by productId AND variantId (if variant exists)
        const existingItem = items.find(
          (item) =>
            item.productId === product.productId &&
            item.variantId === product.variantId
        );

        if (existingItem) {
          // Update quantity if item already exists
          const newQuantity = existingItem.quantity + quantity;

          // Validate against stock
          if (newQuantity > product.stock) {
            throw new Error('Not enough stock available');
          }

          const newItems = items.map((item) =>
            item.productId === product.productId &&
            item.variantId === product.variantId
              ? { ...item, quantity: newQuantity }
              : item
          );

          set({
            items: newItems,
          });
        } else {
          // Add new item
          if (quantity > product.stock) {
            throw new Error('Not enough stock available');
          }

          const newItems = [...items, { ...product, quantity }];

          set({
            items: newItems,
          });
        }
      },

      removeItem: (productId, variantId) => {
        const newItems = get().items.filter(
          (item) =>
            !(item.productId === productId && item.variantId === variantId)
        );
        set({
          items: newItems,
        });
      },

      removeUnavailableItems: (productIds) => {
        if (!productIds || productIds.length === 0) return;

        const productIdSet = new Set(productIds);
        const newItems = get().items.filter(
          (item) => !productIdSet.has(item.productId)
        );
        set({
          items: newItems,
        });
      },

      updateQuantity: (productId, quantity, variantId) => {
        const { items } = get();
        const item = items.find(
          (i) => i.productId === productId && i.variantId === variantId
        );

        if (!item) {
          throw new Error('Cart item was not found');
        }

        // Validate quantity
        if (quantity <= 0) {
          // Remove item if quantity is 0 or negative
          get().removeItem(productId, variantId);
          return;
        }

        if (quantity > item.stock) {
          throw new Error('Not enough stock available');
        }

        const newItems = items.map((i) =>
          i.productId === productId && i.variantId === variantId
            ? { ...i, quantity }
            : i
        );

        set({
          items: newItems,
        });
      },

      clearCart: () => {
        set({ items: [] });
      },

      // These are placeholder values - use selectors below for actual computed values
      total: 0,
      itemCount: 0,
    }),
    {
      name: 'cart-storage',
      // Use browser-safe storage to prevent SSR errors
      storage: createBrowserStorage(),
      // Only persist items, computed values will be recalculated
      partialize: (state) => ({ items: state.items }),
    }
  )
);

/**
 * Selector for computing total from items
 */
export const selectTotal = (state: CartStore) =>
  state.items.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.price * item.quantity, 0);

/**
 * Selector for computing item count from items
 */
export const selectItemCount = (state: CartStore) =>
  state.items.reduce((count, item) => count + item.quantity, 0);

export function formatPrice(price: number): string {
  return formatStorefrontPrice(price);
}

   101	      other: {
   102	        'og:type': 'product',
   103	        'product:price:amount': finalPrice.toString(),
   104	        'product:price:currency': siteLocale.currency,
   105	        'product:availability': product.stock > 0 ? 'in stock' : 'out of stock',
   106	        'product:condition': 'new',
   107	      },
   108	    };
   109	  } catch {
   110	    return {
   111	      title: `Product not found - ${siteConfig.displayName}`,
   112	      description: 'This product is not currently available.',
   113	    };
   114	  }
   115	}
   116	
   117	export default async function ProductDetailPage({ params }: ProductPageProps) {
   118	  const { id } = await params;
   119	  let product;
   120	  let relatedProducts;
   121	
   122	  try {
   123	    product = await getCachedProduct(id);
   124	    // Fetch related products
   125	    relatedProducts = await getRelatedProducts(id, { limit: 4 });
   126	  } catch {
   127	    notFound();
   128	  }
   129	
   130	  // Serialize product data for client component
   131	  type ProductWithRelations = Product & {
   132	    variants?: Array<
   133	      ProductVariant & {
   134	        media?: Array<{
   135	          id: string;
   136	          type: 'IMAGE' | 'VIDEO';
   137	          url: string;
   138	          alt?: string;
   139	          order: number;
   140	        }>;
   141	      }
   142	    >;
   143	    category?: { id: string; name: string; slug: string } | null;
   144	    tags?: Array<{ id: string; name: string; slug: string }>;
   145	    media?: Array<{
   146	      id: string;
   147	      type: 'IMAGE' | 'VIDEO';
   148	      url: string;
   149	      alt?: string;
   150	      order: number;
   151	    }>;
   152	  };
   153	
   154	  const productWithRelations = product as ProductWithRelations;
   155	  const serializedProduct = {
   156	    ...product,
   157	    price: Number(product.price),
   158	    images: product.images || [],
   159	    discountPercent: product.discountPercent,
   160	    hasVariants: product.hasVariants,
   161	    isFeatured: product.isFeatured,
   162	    category: 'category' in product ? productWithRelations.category : null,
   163	    tags: 'tags' in product ? productWithRelations.tags || [] : [],
   164	    media: 'media' in product ? productWithRelations.media || [] : [],
   165	    variants:
   166	      'variants' in product &&
   167	      productWithRelations.variants &&
   168	      Array.isArray(productWithRelations.variants)
   169	        ? productWithRelations.variants.map((v) => ({
   170	            ...v,
   171	            sku: v.sku || undefined,
   172	            color: v.color || undefined,
   173	            size: v.size || undefined,
   174	            material: v.material || undefined,
   175	            priceAdjust: Number(v.priceAdjust),
   176	            media: v.media || [],
   177	          }))
   178	        : [],
   179	  };
   180	
   181	  // Serialize related products for client component
   182	  const serializedRelatedProducts = relatedProducts.map((p) => ({
   183	    id: p.id,
   184	    name: p.name,
   185	    description: p.description,
   186	    price: Number(p.price),
   187	    discountPercent: p.discountPercent,
   188	    stock: p.stock,
   189	    images: p.images || [],
   190	    isActive: p.isActive,
   191	    isFeatured: p.isFeatured,
   192	    hasVariants: p.hasVariants,
   193	    variants: p.variants
   194	      ? p.variants.map((v) => ({
   195	          ...v,
   196	          sku: v.sku || undefined,
   197	          color: v.color || undefined,
   198	          size: v.size || undefined,
   199	          material: v.material || undefined,
   200	          priceAdjust: Number(v.priceAdjust),
   201	          media: v.media || [],
   202	        }))
   203	      : [],
   204	  }));
   205	
   206	  // Generate JSON-LD structured data
   207	  const productSchema = generateProductSchema(productWithRelations);
   208	  const breadcrumbItems = generateProductBreadcrumbs(productWithRelations);
   209	  const breadcrumbSchema = generateBreadcrumbSchema(breadcrumbItems);
   210	
   211	  return (
   212	    <>
   213	      {/* Product JSON-LD structured data */}
   214	      <script
   215	        type="application/ld+json"
   216	        dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: renderJsonLd(productSchema) }}
   217	      />
   218	      {/* Breadcrumb JSON-LD structured data */}
   219	      <script
   220	        type="application/ld+json"
   221	        dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: renderJsonLd(breadcrumbSchema) }}
   222	      />
   223	      <div className="min-h-screen bg-slate-50 pt-16 dark:bg-slate-950">
   224	        <main className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-8 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   225	          <ProductDetail product={serializedProduct} />
   226	          <RelatedProducts products={serializedRelatedProducts} />
   227	        </main>
   228	      </div>
   229	    </>
   230	  );
   231	}
     1	'use client';
     2	
     3	import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
     4	import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
     5	import { MinusIcon, PlusIcon, TagIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
     6	import { useCartStore } from '@/store/cart-store';
     7	import { formatPrice } from '@/lib/utils/format';
     8	import Card from '@/components/ui/Card';
     9	import Button from '@/components/ui/Button';
    10	import ProductGallery from './ProductGallery';
    11	import VariantSelector from './VariantSelector';
    12	
    13	interface MediaItem {
    14	  id: string;
    15	  type: 'IMAGE' | 'VIDEO';
    16	  url: string;
    17	  alt?: string;
    18	  order: number;
    19	}
    20	
    21	interface Variant {
    22	  id: string;
    23	  name: string;
    24	  sku?: string;
    25	  color?: string;
    26	  size?: string;
    27	  material?: string;
    28	  priceAdjust: number;
    29	  stock: number;
    30	  isActive: boolean;
    31	  media?: MediaItem[];
    32	}
    33	
    34	interface Category {
    35	  id: string;
    36	  name: string;
    37	  slug: string;
    38	}
    39	
    40	interface Tag {
    41	  id: string;
    42	  name: string;
    43	  slug: string;
    44	}
    45	
    46	interface ProductDetailProps {
    47	  product: {
    48	    id: string;
    49	    name: string;
    50	    description: string;
    51	    price: number;
    52	    discountPercent?: number | null;
    53	    stock: number;
    54	    images: string[];
    55	    hasVariants?: boolean;
    56	    isActive: boolean;
    57	    isFeatured?: boolean;
    58	    category?: Category | null;
    59	    tags?: Tag[];
    60	    media?: MediaItem[];
    61	    variants?: Variant[];
    62	  };
    63	}
    64	
    65	export default function ProductDetail({ product }: ProductDetailProps) {
    66	  const router = useRouter();
    67	  const addItem = useCartStore((state) => state.addItem);
    68	  const [quantity, setQuantity] = useState(1);
    69	  const [isAdding, setIsAdding] = useState(false);
    70	  const [error, setError] = useState('');
    71	
    72	  // Auto-select first active variant with media if available
    73	  // If product has no product-level media but has variants, auto-select first variant
    74	  const getDefaultVariant = (): Variant | null => {
    75	    if (!product.variants || product.variants.length === 0) return null;
    76	
    77	    const hasProductMedia = product.media && product.media.length > 0;
    78	
    79	    // If product has no product-level media, always select first active variant
    80	    // to ensure images are displayed
    81	    if (!hasProductMedia) {
    82	      const firstActive = product.variants.find((v) => v.isActive);
    83	      return firstActive || null;
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    // Otherwise, prioritize variants with media
    87	    const variantWithMedia = product.variants.find(
    88	      (v) => v.isActive && v.media && v.media.length > 0
    89	    );
    90	    if (variantWithMedia) return variantWithMedia;
    91	
    92	    // Fallback to first active variant
    93	    const firstActive = product.variants.find((v) => v.isActive);
    94	    return firstActive || null;
    95	  };
    96	
    97	  const [selectedVariant, setSelectedVariant] = useState<Variant | null>(() =>
    98	    getDefaultVariant()
    99	  );
   100	
   101	  // Ensure default variant is set when component mounts or product changes
   102	  useEffect(() => {
   103	    if (!product.variants || product.variants.length === 0) return;
   104	
   105	    const hasProductMedia = product.media && product.media.length > 0;
   106	
   107	    let defaultVariant: Variant | null = null;
   108	
   109	    if (!hasProductMedia) {
   110	      defaultVariant = product.variants.find((v) => v.isActive) || null;
   111	    } else {
   112	      const variantWithMedia = product.variants.find(
   113	        (v) => v.isActive && v.media && v.media.length > 0
   114	      );
   115	      defaultVariant =
   116	        variantWithMedia || product.variants.find((v) => v.isActive) || null;
   117	    }
   118	
   119	    if (
   120	      defaultVariant &&
   121	      (!selectedVariant || selectedVariant.id !== defaultVariant.id)
   122	    ) {
   123	      setSelectedVariant(defaultVariant);
   124	    }
   125	    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
   126	  }, [product.id, product.variants, product.media]); // Re-run when product data changes
   127	
   128	  // Calculate discount
   129	  const discountPercent = product.discountPercent || 0;
   130	
   131	  // Calculate effective price and stock based on variant selection
   132	  const basePrice = selectedVariant
   133	    ? product.price + Number(selectedVariant.priceAdjust)
   134	    : product.price;
   135	
   136	  // Apply discount to effective price
   137	  const effectivePrice =
   138	    discountPercent > 0 ? basePrice * (1 - discountPercent / 100) : basePrice;
   139	
   140	  const effectiveStock = selectedVariant
   141	    ? selectedVariant.stock
   142	    : product.stock;
   143	  const isOutOfStock = effectiveStock === 0;
   144	
   145	  const handleIncrement = () => {
   146	    if (quantity < effectiveStock) {
   147	      setQuantity((prev) => prev + 1);
   148	    }
   149	  };
   150	
   151	  const handleDecrement = () => {
   152	    if (quantity > 1) {
   153	      setQuantity((prev) => prev - 1);
   154	    }
   155	  };
   156	
   157	  const handleVariantSelect = (variant: Variant | null) => {
   158	    setSelectedVariant(variant);
   159	    setQuantity(1); // Reset quantity when variant changes
   160	    setError('');
   161	  };
   162	
   163	  const handleAddToCart = async () => {
   164	    try {
   165	      setError('');
   166	
   167	      // If product has variants enabled, variant selection is REQUIRED
   168	      if (product.hasVariants && !selectedVariant) {
   169	        setError('Select a product option first');
   170	        return;
   171	      }
   172	
   173	      setIsAdding(true);
   174	
   175	      // Get the first media URL or fallback to legacy images
   176	      const imageUrl =
   177	        product.media && product.media.length > 0
   178	          ? product.media[0].url
   179	          : product.images && product.images.length > 0
   180	            ? product.images[0]
   181	            : '';
   182	
   183	      addItem(
   184	        {
   185	          productId: product.id,
   186	          name: selectedVariant
   187	            ? `${product.name} - ${selectedVariant.name}`
   188	            : product.name,
   189	          price: effectivePrice,
   190	          image: imageUrl,
   191	          stock: effectiveStock,
   192	          variantId: selectedVariant?.id,
   193	          variantName: selectedVariant?.name,
   194	        },
   195	        quantity
   196	      );
   197	
   198	      // Show success and reset
   199	      setTimeout(() => {
   200	        setIsAdding(false);
   201	        setQuantity(1);
   202	        const shouldCheckout = confirm(
   203	          'Product added to cart. Go to checkout now?'
   204	        );
   205	        if (shouldCheckout) {
   206	          router.push('/checkout');
   207	        }
   208	      }, 300);
   209	    } catch (err) {
   210	      setError(
   211	        err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Could not add product to cart'
   212	      );
   213	      setIsAdding(false);
   214	    }
   215	  };
   216	
   217	  return (
   218	    <>
   219	      {/* Breadcrumb */}
   220	      <div className="mb-6 text-sm">
   221	        <button
   222	          onClick={() => router.push('/products')}
   223	          className="text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-800"
   224	        >
   225	          Products
   226	        </button>
   227	        {product.category && (
   228	          <>
   229	            <span className="mx-2 text-slate-300">/</span>
   230	            <button
   231	              onClick={() =>
   232	                product.category &&
   233	                router.push(`/products?category=${product.category.slug}`)
   234	              }
   235	              className="text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-800"
   236	            >
   237	              {product.category.name}
   238	            </button>
   239	          </>
   240	        )}
   241	        <span className="mx-2 text-slate-300">/</span>
   242	        <span className="text-slate-900 dark:text-slate-100">
   243	          {product.name}
   244	        </span>
   245	      </div>
   246	
   247	      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-8 md:grid-cols-2">
   248	        {/* Product Gallery */}
   249	        <div>
   250	          {product.media && product.media.length > 0 ? (
   251	            <ProductGallery
   252	              media={product.media}
   253	              productName={product.name}
   254	              selectedVariant={selectedVariant}
   255	              allVariants={product.variants}
   256	            />
   257	          ) : selectedVariant &&
   258	            selectedVariant.media &&
   259	            selectedVariant.media.length > 0 ? (
   260	            <ProductGallery
   261	              media={product.media || []}
   262	              productName={product.name}
   263	              selectedVariant={selectedVariant}
   264	              allVariants={product.variants}
   265	            />
   266	          ) : (
   267	            <Card>
   268	              <div className="flex h-96 items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-slate-100 dark:bg-slate-800">
   269	                <div className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-400">
   270	                  No image
   271	                </div>
   272	              </div>
   273	            </Card>
   274	          )}
   275	        </div>
   276	
   277	        {/* Product Details */}
   278	        <div>
   279	          <h1 className="mb-4 text-3xl font-bold text-slate-950 dark:text-white">
   280	            {product.name}
   281	          </h1>
   282	
   283	          {/* Tags */}
   284	          {product.tags && product.tags.length > 0 && (
   285	            <div className="mb-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   286	              {product.tags.map((tag) => (
   287	                <button
   288	                  key={tag.id}
   289	                  onClick={() => router.push(`/products?tag=${tag.slug}`)}
   290	                  className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white px-3 py-1 text-sm text-slate-700 transition-colors hover:bg-slate-50"
   291	                >
   292	                  <TagIcon className="h-3 w-3" />
   293	                  {tag.name}
   294	                </button>
   295	              ))}
   296	            </div>
   297	          )}
   298	
   299	          {/* Price */}
   300	          <div className="mb-6">
   301	            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-wrap">
   302	              {discountPercent > 0 && (
   303	                <span className="text-2xl font-bold text-slate-400 line-through">
   304	                  {formatPrice(basePrice)}
   305	                </span>
   306	              )}
   307	              <span className="text-3xl font-bold text-slate-950 dark:text-white">
   308	                {formatPrice(effectivePrice)}
   309	              </span>
   310	              {discountPercent > 0 && (
   311	                <span className="rounded-full bg-red-100 px-3 py-1 text-sm font-bold text-red-700">
   312	                  {discountPercent}% off
   313	                </span>
   314	              )}
   315	              {product.isFeatured && (
   316	                <span className="rounded-full bg-slate-900 px-3 py-1 text-sm font-bold text-white">
   317	                  Featured
   318	                </span>
   319	              )}
   320	            </div>
   321	            {selectedVariant && selectedVariant.priceAdjust !== 0 && (
   322	              <div className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-500">
   323	                Base price: {formatPrice(product.price)}
   324	                {discountPercent > 0 && (
   325	                  <span className="ml-2">(before discount)</span>
   326	                )}
   327	              </div>
   328	            )}
   329	          </div>
   330	
   331	          {/* Stock Status */}
   332	          <div className="mb-6">
   333	            {isOutOfStock ? (
   334	              <span className="inline-block rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-slate-100 px-4 py-2 font-medium text-slate-600">
   335	                Out of stock
   336	              </span>
   337	            ) : (
   338	              <span className="inline-block rounded-full border border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50 px-4 py-2 font-medium text-emerald-700">
   339	                In stock ({effectiveStock} available)
   340	              </span>
   341	            )}
   342	          </div>
   343	
   344	          {/* Variant Selector */}
   345	          {product.variants && product.variants.length > 0 && (
   346	            <Card className="mb-6">
   347	              <VariantSelector
   348	                variants={product.variants}
   349	                basePrice={product.price}
   350	                onVariantSelect={handleVariantSelect}
   351	                selectedVariantId={selectedVariant?.id}
   352	              />
   353	            </Card>
   354	          )}
   355	
   356	          {/* Description */}
   357	          <Card className="mb-6">
   358	            <h2 className="mb-3 text-xl font-semibold text-slate-950 dark:text-white">
   359	              Product description
   360	            </h2>
   361	            <p className="whitespace-pre-line leading-relaxed text-slate-600 dark:text-slate-400">
   362	              {product.description}
   363	            </p>
   364	          </Card>
   365	
   366	          {/* Error Message */}
   367	          {error && (
   368	            <div className="mb-4 p-3 bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-2xl">
   369	              <p className="text-sm text-amber-700">{error}</p>
   370	            </div>
   371	          )}
   372	
   373	          {/* Quantity Selector */}
   374	          {!isOutOfStock && (
   375	            <div className="mb-6">
   376	              <label className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">
   377	                Quantity
   378	              </label>
   379	              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
   380	                <button
   381	                  onClick={handleDecrement}
   382	                  disabled={quantity <= 1}
   383	                  className="rounded-lg border border-slate-200 p-2 transition-colors hover:bg-slate-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
   384	                  aria-label="Decrease quantity"
   385	                >
   386	                  <MinusIcon className="w-5 h-5 text-slate-600" />
   387	                </button>
   388	
   389	                <span className="text-lg font-medium text-slate-900 min-w-[3rem] text-center">
   390	                  {quantity}
   391	                </span>
   392	
   393	                <button
   394	                  onClick={handleIncrement}
   395	                  disabled={quantity >= effectiveStock}
   396	                  className="rounded-lg border border-slate-200 p-2 transition-colors hover:bg-slate-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
   397	                  aria-label="Increase quantity"
   398	                >
   399	                  <PlusIcon className="w-5 h-5 text-slate-600" />
   400	                </button>
   401	
   402	                {quantity >= effectiveStock && (
   403	                  <span className="ml-2 text-sm text-amber-600">
   404	                    Maximum stock
   405	                  </span>
   406	                )}
   407	              </div>
   408	            </div>
   409	          )}
   410	
   411	          {/* Add to Cart */}
   412	          <div className="space-y-4">
   413	            <Button
   414	              variant="primary"
   415	              size="lg"
   416	              className="w-full"
   417	              disabled={isOutOfStock}
   418	              isLoading={isAdding}
   419	              onClick={handleAddToCart}
   420	            >
   421	              {isOutOfStock
   422	                ? 'Out of stock'
   423	                : isAdding
   424	                  ? 'Adding...'
   425	                  : 'Add to Cart'}
   426	            </Button>
   427	
   428	            <Button
   429	              variant="secondary"
   430	              size="lg"
   431	              className="w-full"
   432	              onClick={() => router.back()}
   433	            >
   434	              Back to products
   435	            </Button>
   436	          </div>
   437	        </div>
   438	      </div>
   439	    </>
   440	  );
   441	}
