@@ -427,7 +431,7 @@ export default function ProductDetail({ product }: ProductDetailProps) {
               className="w-full"
     1	'use client';
     2	
     3	import { useState, useEffect, useMemo, useRef } from 'react';
     4	import Image from 'next/image';
     5	import {
     6	  ChevronLeftIcon,
     7	  ChevronRightIcon,
     8	  XMarkIcon,
     9	} from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
    10	import { PlayIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/solid';
    11	import { optimizeImage } from '@/lib/cloudflare-images-client';
    12	import { generateProductAltText } from '@/lib/seo/alt-text';
    13	
    14	interface MediaItem {
    15	  id: string;
    16	  type: 'IMAGE' | 'VIDEO';
    17	  url: string;
    18	  alt?: string;
    19	  order: number;
    20	  variantId?: string | null;
    21	}
    22	
    23	interface Variant {
    24	  id: string;
    25	  name?: string;
    26	  color?: string | null;
    27	  size?: string | null;
    28	  material?: string | null;
    29	  media?: MediaItem[];
    30	}
    31	
    32	interface ProductGalleryProps {
    33	  media: MediaItem[];
    34	  productName: string;
    35	  selectedVariant?: Variant | null;
    36	  allVariants?: Variant[]; // NEW: All product variants for aggressive preloading
    37	}
    38	
    39	export default function ProductGallery({
    40	  media,
    41	  productName,
    42	  selectedVariant,
    43	  allVariants,
    44	}: ProductGalleryProps) {
    45	  const [selectedIndex, setSelectedIndex] = useState(0);
    46	  const [isZoomed, setIsZoomed] = useState(false);
    47	  const [isTransitioning, setIsTransitioning] = useState(false);
    48	
    49	  // Track preloaded variant IDs to avoid redundant preloading
    50	  const preloadedVariants = useRef<Set<string>>(new Set());
    51	
    52	  // Touch swipe handling (for main gallery)
    53	  const touchStartX = useRef<number>(0);
    54	  const touchEndX = useRef<number>(0);
    55	  const minSwipeDistance = 50; // Minimum swipe distance in pixels
    56	
    57	  // Touch swipe handling (for zoom modal)
    58	  const zoomTouchStartX = useRef<number>(0);
    59	  const zoomTouchEndX = useRef<number>(0);
    60	
    61	  // Memoize filtered and sorted media to avoid recalculating on every render
    62	  const sortedMedia = useMemo(() => {
    63	    let displayMedia: MediaItem[];
    64	
    65	    if (!selectedVariant) {
    66	      // Show only product-level media (no variantId) when no variant is selected
    67	      displayMedia = media.filter((m) => !m.variantId);
    68	    } else {
    69	      // When variant is selected, prefer variant-specific media
    70	      const variantMedia = selectedVariant.media || [];
    71	
    72	      // If variant has no specific media, fall back to product-level media
    73	      displayMedia =
    74	        variantMedia.length === 0
    75	          ? media.filter((m) => !m.variantId)
    76	          : variantMedia;
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    // Sort by order
    80	    return [...displayMedia].sort((a, b) => a.order - b.order);
    81	  }, [media, selectedVariant]);
    82	
    83	  // STRATEGY 1: Preload current variant/product images IMMEDIATELY when sortedMedia changes
    84	  useEffect(() => {
    85	    // Mark current variant as preloaded
    86	    const variantKey = selectedVariant?.id || 'product-default';
    87	
    88	    // Preload first 5 images for instant switching
    89	    sortedMedia.slice(0, 5).forEach((item, index) => {
    90	      if (item.type === 'IMAGE') {
    91	        const img = new window.Image();
    92	        // Use large variant for main gallery
    93	        img.src = optimizeImage.large(item.url);
    94	
    95	        // Also preload thumbnail for gallery thumbnails
    96	        const thumbImg = new window.Image();
    97	        thumbImg.src = optimizeImage.adminThumb(item.url);
    98	
    99	        // Set loading priority - first 3 images are high priority
   100	        if (index < 3) {
   101	          img.fetchPriority = 'high';
   102	          thumbImg.fetchPriority = 'high';
   103	        }
   104	      }
   105	    });
   106	
   107	    preloadedVariants.current.add(variantKey);
   108	  }, [sortedMedia, selectedVariant?.id]);
   109	
   110	  // STRATEGY 2: Aggressively preload ALL variant images on component mount
   111	  // This ensures instant switching even before user selects a variant
   112	  useEffect(() => {
   113	    const allMediaToPreload: MediaItem[] = [];
   114	    const seenUrls = new Set<string>(); // Avoid duplicate preloads
   115	
   116	    // 1. Add product-level media (highest priority - shown by default)
   117	    const productMedia = media.filter((m) => !m.variantId);
   118	    productMedia.forEach((item) => {
   119	      if (item.type === 'IMAGE' && !seenUrls.has(item.url)) {
   120	        allMediaToPreload.push({ ...item, priority: 1 } as MediaItem & {
   121	          priority: number;
   122	        });
   123	        seenUrls.add(item.url);
   124	      }
   125	    });
   126	
   127	    // 2. Add ALL variants' media (preload to enable instant switching)
   128	    if (allVariants && allVariants.length > 0) {
   129	      allVariants.forEach((variant) => {
   130	        if (variant.media && variant.media.length > 0) {
   131	          variant.media.forEach((item, itemIndex) => {
   132	            if (item.type === 'IMAGE' && !seenUrls.has(item.url)) {
   133	              // First image of each variant gets higher priority
   134	              const priority = itemIndex === 0 ? 2 : 3;
   135	              allMediaToPreload.push({ ...item, priority } as MediaItem & {
   136	                priority: number;
   137	              });
   138	              seenUrls.add(item.url);
   139	            }
   140	          });
   141	        }
   142	      });
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    // Define extended type for preload items
   146	    type PreloadItem = MediaItem & { priority: number };
   147	
   148	    // 3. Sort by priority (1 = highest, 3 = lowest) and preload
   149	    allMediaToPreload
   150	      .sort((a, b) => (a as PreloadItem).priority - (b as PreloadItem).priority)
   151	      .forEach((item, index) => {
   152	        const priority = (item as PreloadItem).priority;
   153	        const isHighPriority = priority === 1 || index === 0;
   154	
   155	        // Use requestIdleCallback for low-priority images to avoid blocking
   156	        const preloadFn = () => {
   157	          const img = new window.Image();
   158	          img.src = optimizeImage.large(item.url);
   159	          if (isHighPriority) {
   160	            img.fetchPriority = 'high';
   161	          }
   162	
   163	          // Also preload thumbnail
   164	          const thumbImg = new window.Image();
   165	          thumbImg.src = optimizeImage.adminThumb(item.url);
   166	          if (isHighPriority) {
   167	            thumbImg.fetchPriority = 'high';
   168	          }
   169	        };
   170	
   171	        if (isHighPriority) {
   172	          // Load high-priority images immediately
   173	          preloadFn();
   174	        } else {
   175	          // Load low-priority images during idle time
   176	          if (
   177	            typeof window !== 'undefined' &&
   178	            'requestIdleCallback' in window
   179	          ) {
   180	            window.requestIdleCallback(preloadFn);
   181	          } else {
   182	            // Fallback: use setTimeout to defer loading
   183	            setTimeout(preloadFn, 100);
   184	          }
   185	        }
   186	      });
   187	  }, [media, allVariants]); // Run once when component mounts or media/variants change
   188	
   189	  // Reset selectedIndex when variant changes or media changes
   190	  useEffect(() => {
   191	    setSelectedIndex(0);
   192	    setIsZoomed(false);
   193	  }, [selectedVariant?.id, media.length]);
   194	
   195	  // Handle ESC key to close zoom modal and prevent body scroll
   196	  useEffect(() => {
   197	    const handleKeyDown = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
   198	      if (e.key === 'Escape' && isZoomed) {
   199	        setIsZoomed(false);
   200	      }
   201	    };
   202	
   203	    if (isZoomed) {
   204	      // Prevent body scroll when modal is open
   205	      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
   206	      window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
   207	    } else {
   208	      document.body.style.overflow = '';
   209	    }
   210	
   211	    return () => {
   212	      document.body.style.overflow = '';
   213	      window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
   214	    };
   215	  }, [isZoomed]);
   216	
   217	  if (!sortedMedia || sortedMedia.length === 0) {
   218	    return (
   219	      <div className="w-full aspect-square bg-gray-200 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center">
   220	        <p className="text-gray-400">No image available</p>
   221	      </div>
   222	    );
   223	  }
   224	
   225	  const currentMedia = sortedMedia[selectedIndex];
   226	
   227	  const goToPrevious = () => {
   228	    setIsTransitioning(true);
   229	    setSelectedIndex((prev) =>
   230	      prev === 0 ? sortedMedia.length - 1 : prev - 1
   231	    );
   232	    // Brief transition effect, then reset
   233	    setTimeout(() => {
   234	      setIsTransitioning(false);
   235	    }, 100);
   236	  };
   237	
   238	  const goToNext = () => {
   239	    setIsTransitioning(true);
   240	    setSelectedIndex((prev) =>
   241	      prev === sortedMedia.length - 1 ? 0 : prev + 1
   242	    );
   243	    // Brief transition effect, then reset
   244	    setTimeout(() => {
   245	      setIsTransitioning(false);
   246	    }, 100);
   247	  };
   248	
   249	  const handleThumbnailClick = (index: number) => {
   250	    if (index !== selectedIndex) {
   251	      setIsTransitioning(true);
   252	      setSelectedIndex(index);
   253	      // Brief transition effect, then reset
   254	      setTimeout(() => {
   255	        setIsTransitioning(false);
   256	      }, 100);
   257	    }
   258	    setIsZoomed(false);
   259	  };
   260	
   261	  // Touch swipe handlers for main gallery
   262	  const onTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   263	    touchEndX.current = 0; // Reset
   264	    touchStartX.current = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
   265	  };
   266	
   267	  const onTouchMove = (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   268	    touchEndX.current = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
   269	  };
   270	
   271	  const onTouchEnd = () => {
   272	    if (!touchStartX.current || !touchEndX.current) return;
   273	
   274	    const distance = touchStartX.current - touchEndX.current;
   275	    const isLeftSwipe = distance > minSwipeDistance;
   276	    const isRightSwipe = distance < -minSwipeDistance;
   277	
   278	    // In RTL, left swipe = previous, right swipe = next
   279	    if (isLeftSwipe) {
   280	      goToPrevious();
   281	    } else if (isRightSwipe) {
   282	      goToNext();
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    // Reset
   286	    touchStartX.current = 0;
   287	    touchEndX.current = 0;
   288	  };
   289	
   290	  // Touch swipe handlers for zoom modal
   291	  const onZoomTouchStart = (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   292	    zoomTouchEndX.current = 0; // Reset
   293	    zoomTouchStartX.current = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
   294	  };
   295	
   296	  const onZoomTouchMove = (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   297	    zoomTouchEndX.current = e.targetTouches[0].clientX;
   298	  };
   299	
   300	  const onZoomTouchEnd = (e: React.TouchEvent) => {
   301	    e.stopPropagation(); // Prevent closing modal on swipe
   302	
   303	    if (!zoomTouchStartX.current || !zoomTouchEndX.current) return;
   304	
   305	    const distance = zoomTouchStartX.current - zoomTouchEndX.current;
   306	    const isLeftSwipe = distance > minSwipeDistance;
   307	    const isRightSwipe = distance < -minSwipeDistance;
   308	
   309	    // In RTL, left swipe = previous, right swipe = next
   310	    if (isLeftSwipe) {
   311	      goToPrevious();
   312	    } else if (isRightSwipe) {
   313	      goToNext();
   314	    }
   315	
   316	    // Reset
   317	    zoomTouchStartX.current = 0;
   318	    zoomTouchEndX.current = 0;
   319	  };
   320

'use client';

export { default } from '../ui-v4/Badge';
export type { BadgeV4Props as BadgeProps } from '../ui-v4/Badge';
'use client';

import { ReactNode, forwardRef, HTMLAttributes } from 'react';

export interface BadgeV4Props extends HTMLAttributes<HTMLSpanElement> {
  variant?:
    | 'default'
    | 'outline'
    | 'success'
    | 'warning'
    | 'error'
    | 'info'
    | 'premium';
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  dot?: boolean;
  pulse?: boolean;
  children: ReactNode;
}

const BadgeV4 = forwardRef<HTMLSpanElement, BadgeV4Props>(
  (
    {
      variant = 'default',
      size = 'md',
      dot = false,
      pulse = false,
      children,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const baseStyles = `
      inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5
      font-medium
      rounded-full
      whitespace-nowrap
      transition-all duration-200
    `;

    const variantStyles = {
      default: 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 border border-slate-200',
      outline: 'bg-transparent border border-slate-300 text-slate-600',
      success: 'bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700 border border-emerald-200',
      warning: 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-700 border border-amber-200',
      error: 'bg-red-100 text-red-700 border border-red-200',
      info: 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 border border-blue-200',
      premium: 'bg-slate-900 text-white border border-slate-900',
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      sm: 'h-5 px-2 text-[11px]',
      md: 'h-6 px-3 text-xs',
      lg: 'h-7 px-4 text-sm',
    };

    const dotColors = {
      default: 'bg-slate-500',
      outline: 'bg-slate-400',
      success: 'bg-emerald-500',
      warning: 'bg-amber-500',
      error: 'bg-red-500',
      info: 'bg-blue-500',
      premium: 'bg-white',
    };

    return (
      <span
        ref={ref}
        className={`
          ${baseStyles}
          ${variantStyles[variant]}
          ${sizeStyles[size]}
          ${className}
        `}
        {...props}
      >
        {dot && (
          <span className="relative flex h-2 w-2">
            {pulse && (
              <span
                className={`absolute inline-flex h-full w-full rounded-full ${dotColors[variant]} opacity-75 animate-ping`}
              />
            )}
            <span
              className={`relative inline-flex rounded-full h-2 w-2 ${dotColors[variant]}`}
            />
          </span>
        )}
        {children}
      </span>
    );
  }
);

BadgeV4.displayName = 'BadgeV4';

export default BadgeV4;

--- tasks/task-009.md
# Task 009 - Test Suite Migration and Local Verification

## Goal
Update tests to match new schema and payment architecture, then verify locally.

## Scope
- Remove or rewrite OTP/Kavenegar/legacy gateway tests.
- Add Stripe/PayPal focused unit/integration tests.
- Keep CI deterministic via mocks where needed.

## Steps
1. Replace legacy gateway fixtures and mocks.
2. Remove `otp_verifications` test setup/cleanup logic.
3. Add webhook idempotency tests for both providers.
4. Add contract tests for transaction state transitions.
5. Run local test matrix and capture known failures.

## Edge Cases
- Flaky tests due to webhook timing/race conditions.
- Tests accidentally using production credentials.
- Snapshot tests tied to old Persian labels for removed methods.

## Acceptance Criteria
- No tests reference removed columns or OTP table.
- Critical payment flow tests pass locally.
- CI config includes required Stripe/PayPal test env vars.

## Rollback
- Temporarily mark non-critical flaky tests and keep payment core tests as blocking.

## Completion Notes (2026-02-07)
- Status: Completed
- Completed implementation:
  - Replaced legacy payment verification coverage with Stripe/PayPal suites:
    - added `tests/unit/api/transactions/webhook-stripe.test.ts`.
    - added `tests/unit/api/transactions/webhook-paypal.test.ts`.
    - rewrote `tests/integration/payment-verification.test.ts` for Stripe/PayPal idempotency behavior.
  - Removed obsolete OTP/legacy gateway tests that no longer match runtime routes/services:
    - deleted `tests/unit/api/auth/send-otp.test.ts`.
    - deleted `tests/unit/api/auth/verify-otp.test.ts`.
    - deleted `tests/unit/api/auth/checkout-verify-otp.test.ts`.
    - deleted `tests/unit/api/user/reset-password-otp.test.ts`.

# task009: Public Storefront Redesign

Status: Implementation complete; review rerun blocked by concurrent broad diff traversal

## Goal

Replace the Kitia-specific public storefront with a neutral, boilerplate-quality storefront using the new design system.

## Start Here

- `src/components/layout/Header.tsx`
- `src/components/layout/Footer.tsx`

## Requirements

- Redesign public pages to be neutral and reusable by any commerce project.
- Remove Kitia product/category assumptions, CDN hero images, social links, Telegram/Instagram references, Persian shipping/policy specifics, and charity/brand-specific claims.
- Keep the app usable as the first screen; do not turn it into a marketing-only landing page.
- Product listing, product detail, cart, wishlist, and search should remain functional.
- Use neutral placeholder copy and imagery strategy. If real demo images are needed, use configurable sample image URLs or local placeholders.
- Keep layout responsive and usable on mobile and desktop.
- Use shared formatting utilities for price/currency.

## Acceptance Criteria

- Public storefront contains no Kitia branding, private social links, Persian text, or private CDN URLs.
- Header/footer are neutral and configurable.
- Product, cart, and wishlist flows still use existing data contracts.
- Responsive layout has no obvious overlapping text or controls.

- `npm run verify`
- `npm run lint`

  padding?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
}

  children,
  className = '',

}: CardProps) {

    lg: 'p-8',

'use client';

import { Fragment, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import Image from 'next/image';
import { Combobox, Transition } from '@headlessui/react';
import { MagnifyingGlassIcon, XMarkIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/outline';
import { FolderIcon, TagIcon } from '@heroicons/react/24/solid';
import type { SearchResult } from '@/types/search';
import { formatPrice } from '@/lib/utils/format';

interface SearchBarProps {
  className?: string;
  placeholder?: string;
  onResultClick?: () => void;
}

interface SearchResponse {
  products: Array<SearchResult & { type: 'product' }>;
  categories: Array<SearchResult & { type: 'category' }>;
  total: number;
}

export default function SearchBar({
  className = '',
  placeholder = 'Search products and categories...',
  onResultClick,
}: SearchBarProps) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const [results, setResults] = useState<SearchResponse>({
    products: [],
    categories: [],
    total: 0,
  });
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<SearchResult | null | undefined>(
    null
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    const delayDebounceFn = setTimeout(async () => {
      const trimmedQuery = query.trim();
      if (trimmedQuery.length === 0) {
        setResults({ products: [], categories: [], total: 0 });
        return;
      }

      if (trimmedQuery.length < 2) {
        return;
      }

      setIsLoading(true);
      try {
        const response = await fetch(
          `/api/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(trimmedQuery)}&limit=5`
        );
        const data = await response.json();
        setResults(data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Search error:', error);
        setResults({ products: [], categories: [], total: 0 });
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    }, 300);

    return () => clearTimeout(delayDebounceFn);
  }, [query]);

  const handleSelect = (result: SearchResult | null | undefined) => {
    if (!result) return;

    setSelected(result);

    if (result.type === 'product') {
      router.push(`/products/${result.id}`);
    } else if (result.type === 'category') {
      router.push(`/products?category=${result.slug}`);
    }

    setQuery('');
    setResults({ products: [], categories: [], total: 0 });
    onResultClick?.();
  };

  const allResults: SearchResult[] = [
    ...results.categories,
    ...results.products,
  ];

  const hasResults = allResults.length > 0;

  return (
    <div className={`relative w-full ${className}`}>
      <Combobox value={selected} onChange={handleSelect}>
        <div className="relative">
          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-y-0 start-0 flex items-center ps-3">
            {isLoading ? (
              <div className="h-5 w-5 animate-spin text-slate-400 dark:text-slate-500">
                <svg className="h-5 w-5" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                  <circle
                    className="opacity-25"
                    cx="12"
                    cy="12"
                    r="10"
                    stroke="currentColor"
                    strokeWidth="4"
                  />
                  <path
                    className="opacity-75"
                    fill="currentColor"
                    d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
                  />
                </svg>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <MagnifyingGlassIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-slate-400 dark:text-slate-500" />
            )}
          </div>

          <Combobox.Input
            className="w-full rounded-lg border border-slate-200 bg-white py-2.5 ps-10 pe-10 text-sm text-slate-900 placeholder:text-slate-400 transition-all focus:border-transparent focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-200 dark:border-slate-700 dark:bg-slate-900 dark:text-slate-100 dark:placeholder:text-slate-500 dark:focus:ring-slate-700/60"
            placeholder={placeholder}
            value={query}
            onChange={(event) => setQuery(event.target.value)}
            displayValue={() => query}
          />

          {query && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => {
                setQuery('');
                setResults({ products: [], categories: [], total: 0 });
              }}
              className="absolute inset-y-0 end-0 flex items-center rounded-e-lg pe-3 transition-colors hover:bg-slate-100 dark:hover:bg-slate-800"
              aria-label="Clear search"
            >
              <XMarkIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-600 dark:text-slate-500 dark:hover:text-slate-200" />
            </button>
          )}

          <Transition
            as={Fragment}
            leave="transition ease-in duration-100"
            leaveFrom="opacity-100"
            leaveTo="opacity-0"
            afterLeave={() => setQuery('')}
          >
            <Combobox.Options className="absolute z-50 mt-2 max-h-96 w-full overflow-auto rounded-lg border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-lg focus:outline-none dark:border-slate-800 dark:bg-slate-900 dark:shadow-none">
              {hasResults ? (
                <div className="py-2">
                  {results.categories.length > 0 && (
                    <div className="mb-2">
                      <div className="bg-slate-50 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wide text-slate-500 dark:bg-slate-900/70 dark:text-slate-400">
                        Categories
                      </div>
                      {results.categories.map((category) => (
                        <Combobox.Option
                          key={category.id}
                          value={category}
                          className={({ active }) =>
                            `cursor-pointer select-none px-4 py-3 transition-colors ${
                              active
                                ? 'bg-slate-50 text-slate-950 dark:bg-slate-800 dark:text-slate-100'
                                : 'text-slate-800 dark:text-slate-200'
                            }`
                          }
                        >
                          {({ active }) => (
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                              <div
                                className={`flex h-10 w-10 flex-shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-lg ${
                                  active
                                    ? 'bg-slate-200 dark:bg-slate-700'
                                    : 'bg-slate-100 dark:bg-slate-800'
                                }`}
                              >
                                <FolderIcon className="h-5 w-5 text-slate-500 dark:text-slate-300" />
                              </div>
                              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                                <p className="truncate font-medium">
                                  {category.name}
                                </p>
                                {category.description && (
                                  <p className="mt-0.5 truncate text-xs text-slate-500">
                                    {category.description}
                                  </p>
                                )}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          )}
                        </Combobox.Option>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {results.products.length > 0 && (
                    <div>
                      <div className="bg-slate-50 px-3 py-2 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wide text-slate-500 dark:bg-slate-900/70 dark:text-slate-400">
                        Products
                      </div>
                      {results.products.map((product) => (
                        <Combobox.Option
                          key={product.id}
                          value={product}
                          className={({ active }) =>
                            `cursor-pointer select-none px-4 py-3 transition-colors ${
                              active
                                ? 'bg-slate-50 text-slate-950 dark:bg-slate-800 dark:text-slate-100'
                                : 'text-slate-800 dark:text-slate-200'
                            }`
                          }
                        >
                          {() => (
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                              <div className="relative h-12 w-12 flex-shrink-0 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-slate-200 dark:border-slate-700">
                                {product.images && product.images.length > 0 ? (
                                  <Image
                                    src={product.images[0]}
                                    alt={product.name}
                                    fill
                                    className="object-cover"
                                    sizes="48px"
                                  />
                                ) : (
                                  <div className="flex h-full w-full items-center justify-center bg-slate-100 dark:bg-slate-800">
                                    <TagIcon className="h-6 w-6 text-slate-400 dark:text-slate-500" />
                                  </div>
                                )}
                              </div>

                              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                                <p className="truncate font-medium">
                                  {product.name}
                                </p>
                                <div className="mt-1 flex items-center gap-2">
                                  <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900 dark:text-slate-100">
                                    {formatPrice(product.price)}
                                  </span>
                                  {product.categoryName && (
                                    <>
                                      <span className="text-slate-300 dark:text-slate-600">
                                        |
                                      </span>
                                      <span className="truncate text-xs text-slate-500">
                                        {product.categoryName}
                                      </span>
                                    </>
                                  )}
                                </div>
                              </div>

                              {product.discountPercent &&
                                product.discountPercent > 0 && (
                                  <span className="inline-flex flex-shrink-0 items-center rounded-full bg-red-100 px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-red-700 dark:bg-slate-800 dark:text-slate-200">
                                    {product.discountPercent}% off
                                  </span>
                                )}

exec
/bin/bash -lc "sed -n '260,520p' src/components/ui/SearchBar.tsx" in /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack
 succeeded in 0ms:
                                )}
                            </div>
                          )}
                        </Combobox.Option>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              ) : (
                query.trim().length >= 2 &&
                !isLoading && (
                  <div className="px-4 py-8 text-center text-slate-500 dark:text-slate-400">
                    <MagnifyingGlassIcon className="mx-auto mb-3 h-12 w-12 text-slate-300 dark:text-slate-600" />
                    <p className="text-sm font-medium">No results found</p>
                    <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-400 dark:text-slate-500">
                      Try a different product name or category.
                    </p>
                  </div>
                )
              )}
            </Combobox.Options>
          </Transition>
        </div>
      </Combobox>
    </div>
  );
}
